# Fault Localization: iwlwifi Missing PCI Subdevice Entries

- **Repository**: github.com/sg-evals/linux--11a48a5a (mirror of github.com/sg-evals)/linux--11a48a5a (mirror of torvalds/linux)
- **Kernel Version**: 5.6-rc2
- **Difficulty**: expert
- **Category**: fault_localization
- **Subsystem**: Drivers
- **Component**: network-wireless (Intel iwlwifi)

## Bug Report

**Bug ID**: 206661
**Summary**: iwlwifi:9260: missing PCI subdevice entries for 0x2526 (0x04010, 0x4018 and 0x401C)
**Regression**: Yes

I am using Kernel 5.6 RC2 and I am seeing issues where firmware is not being loaded for my Intel Corporation Wireless-AC 9260 card. Attached is the boot logging.

If I can do anything to debug, let me know.

## Task

You are a fault localization agent. Given the bug report above, your task is to identify the **exact source file(s)** and **function(s)/data structure(s)** in the Linux kernel source tree (at `/workspace`) that need to be modified to fix this bug.

You must:
1. Analyze the bug report to understand the symptoms and context
2. Search the kernel source code to identify the relevant subsystem and files
3. Narrow down to the specific file(s) and function(s)/data structure(s) that contain the bug or need modification
4. Write your findings to `/workspace/fault_localization_result.json` in the following format:

```json
{
  "buggy_files": ["path/to/file.c"],
  "buggy_functions": ["function_or_struct_name"],
  "confidence": 0.8,
  "reasoning": "Brief explanation of why these locations are the fault"
}
```

**Important**: Paths should be relative to the kernel source root (e.g., `kernel/sched/core.c`, not `/workspace/kernel/sched/core.c`).

## Success Criteria

- [ ] Correctly identify the buggy file(s)
- [ ] Correctly identify the buggy function(s) or data structure(s)
- [ ] Write results to `/workspace/fault_localization_result.json`
- [ ] Provide reasoning for the localization

77-assistanttext-
Perfect! My analysis is confirmed. Let me create a summary of my findings:

## Summary

I have successfully localized the fault in the Linux kernel iwlwifi driver. Here are my findings:

### **Buggy File:**
`drivers/net/wireless/intel/iwlwifi/pcie/drv.c`

### **Buggy Data Structure:**
`iwl_dev_info_table` (static const array at lines 978-997)

### **Issue:**
The `iwl_dev_info_table` is missing PCI subdevice entries for Intel Wireless-AC 9260 (device ID 0x2526) with the following subdevice IDs:
- **0x0401**
- **0x4018**
- **0x401C**

### **Root Cause:**
The `iwl_pci_probe()` function (lines 1031-1042) iterates through `iwl_dev_info_table` to match device/subdevice combinations with their corresponding driver configurations. When a device with 0x2526 and one of the missing subdevice IDs is detected, no matching entry is found in the table. This causes the device to not receive the proper 160MHz-capable configuration, resulting in firmware loading failures.

### **Why This is Critical:**
While a catch-all entry exists at line 599 (`IWL_PCI_DEVICE(0x2526, PCI_ANY_ID, iwl9000_trans_cfg)`), this provides only basic configuration. The specific `iwl_dev_info_table` entries are necessary to assign the 160MHz-capable configurations (iwl9260_2ac_160_cfg and iwl9560_2ac_160_cfg) that these devices require.

The result has been written to `/workspace/fault_localization_result.json` with high confidence (0.95).

        Code Changes (1)
        
1. WRITE /workspace/fault_localization_result.json
{
  "buggy_files": ["drivers/net/wireless/intel/iwlwifi/pcie/drv.c"],
  "buggy_functions": ["iwl_dev_info_table"],
  "confidence": 0.95,
  "reasoning": "The bug report indicates missing PCI subdevice entries for Intel Wireless-AC 9260 (device ID 0x2526) with subdevice IDs 0x0401, 0x4018, and 0x401C. These entries are missing from the `iwl_dev_info_table` static array (lines 978-997) in drv.c. This table is used by the iwl_pci_probe() function (lines 1031-1042) to match device/subdevice combinations to their corresponding driver configurations. Without these entries in iwl_dev_info_table, devices with these specific subdevice IDs cannot get proper configuration assignments, resulting in firmware loading failures. While a catch-all entry (line 599: IWL_PCI_DEVICE(0x2526, PCI_ANY_ID, iwl9000_trans_cfg)) exists in iwl_hw_card_ids to detect the device, the more specific iwl_dev_info_table entries are needed for proper configuration matching. The missing entries should include: (0x2526, 0x0401, iwl9260_2ac_160_cfg), (0x2526, 0x4018, iwl9560_2ac_160_cfg), and (0x2526, 0x401C, iwl9560_2ac_160_cfg) based on the patterns of similar subdevice IDs in the table."
}
